- Current holistic ASM audit follow-up (2026-04-26): no cross-file bug accepted from the holistic pass, and no code change was made. Rejected the proposed `_is_ignored()` shrink in `50_main_output.asm`: after `_st_stricmp_cleanup`, the loop restores `HL=nick`, `DE=list_ptr`, and `BC=count`; the suggested `ex de,hl / ld de,16 / add hl,de / ex de,hl` does advance `DE` by 16 but leaves `HL=16`, so the next loop iteration would `push hl` as the nick argument and compare against address `$0010`. The existing byte-wise `DE += 16` keeps `HL=nick` live for the next iteration and is the safe shape. - Current UTF-8 Latin-1 accent verification (2026-04-26): checked `_utf8_to_ascii()` C2/C3 handling after the page-carry fix. The current `SpecTalkZX.map` places `u8a_tbl_c0` at `$D3D9`, so the 64-byte C3 table crosses `$D400`; the repaired carry propagation is therefore required for all higher C3 entries, not only `ñ`. Common accented vowels now read their intended table entries and are deliberately folded to base ASCII (`áéíóú` -> `aeiou`, `ÁÉÍÓÚ` -> `AEIOU`, `ü/Ü` -> `u/U`, `ç/Ç` -> `c/C`). Only `Ñ/ñ` has a display-only custom glyph, mapped to internal byte `127`; inverted punctuation and quotes are normalized (`¡` -> `!`, `¿` -> `?`, `«/»` -> `</>`, smart quotes -> ASCII quotes).
- Current UTF-8/ñ regression fix (2026-04-25): `make` passes at `35727B` trimmed / `35807B` TAP / `407B` BSS slack; overlays are `SPCTLK1/2/3/4 = 2019/2037/1853/2041`. Root cause: recent resident shrinks moved `u8a_tbl_c0` to `$D3D6`, breaking `_utf8_to_ascii()`'s old low-byte-only `add a,l / ld l,a` lookup for C3 Latin-1. For `ñ` (`C3 B1`, index `$31`) the lookup wrapped to `$D307` instead of `$D407`, so `Ñ/ñ` and other C3 accented characters mapped to garbage. Fix: `u8a_c3` now propagates the carry into `H` after `add a,l`, making the table lookup layout-safe. Verified generated `build/SPECTALK.DAT` still patches glyph slot 127 as packed bytes `47 66 66`.

- Current overlay sizes: `SPCTLK1.OVL` 1396B, `SPCTLK2.OVL` 2037B, `SPCTLK3.OVL` 1593B, `SPCTLK4.OVL` 1986B.
- Aggressive shrink experiment status (2026-04-24): shrink-only build after `/channels`, `/theme`, and `main_print()` ASM reached `35394B` trimmed / `35474B` TAP / `838B` slack. The current render/scroll experiment plus the BPE guard in ASM `main_print()` spends some of that cushion, leaving `752B` slack. Rejected probes during this session: earlier `_print_line64_fast()` empty-pair shapes (+19B and +36B before the final broader implementation), fixed-address `cfg_vp` (+26B CODE for only 2B BSS slack), ASM `check_status()` (-4B only for command-precondition risk), and direct pagination `notif_draw(15, ...)` (+4B). Do not retry those exact shapes unless a new structure changes the byte economics.
- Current shrink highlight: before the bookmark feature, the three sequential resident ASM shrink passes (`50`, `70`, `80`) had recovered the tree to `36008B` trimmed / `217B` slack. The independent autojoin refinement spends most of that cushion, leaving `45B` BSS slack; do not add further resident polish on this branch without another shrink pass. The earlier raw-partial-preserve overlay experiment remains rejected because it leaked chopped flood lines on exit; keep the helper-based overlay-exit path.
- Shrink-z80 target selection (2026-04-23): run the next full resident ASM shrink pass first on `asm/spectalk_asm/50_main_output.asm`, then `asm/spectalk_asm/70_input_lookup.asm`; use `asm/spectalk_asm/80_ui_runtime.asm` only as the third target if those stall. Evidence from the scan: `50_main_output.asm` has the known `main_print_wrapped_ram()` IX last-space tracker tax plus BPE/newline tail opportunities, while `70_input_lookup.asm` has a larger approx map span and many independent state machines/saltos. Deprioritize `30_rendering.asm` and `40_text_numeric_screen.asm` for this pass despite their size because they were recently mined and are visual/layout-sensitive.
- First `50_main_output.asm` shrink-z80 pass (2026-04-23): recovered 53 resident bytes (`36135B -> 36082B`) while keeping overlays unchanged. Main wins were replacing the `IX` last-space tracker with transient `$5BE7` scratch, sharing the inline-space clear loop, low-byte BPE stack bounds, `main_col` reuse, and `_st_stricmp_cleanup`. Remaining `jp mpwr_loop` backedge is still just out of `jr` range; do not force it without another measured local shrink.
- Second `70_input_lookup.asm` shrink-z80 pass (2026-04-23): recovers 40 resident bytes (`36082B -> 36042B`) while keeping overlays unchanged. Main wins are UTF-8 skip-chain sharing plus closer `u8a_done`, C3 table low-byte indexing, SNTP scan push/pop removal, shared zero returns in `_read_key()`, low-byte nav-history indexing, and `_st_stricmp_cleanup` reuse in `_find_query()`.
- Third `80_ui_runtime.asm` shrink-z80 pass (2026-04-24): recovers 34 resident bytes (`36042B -> 36008B`) while keeping overlays unchanged. Main wins are compacting `_in_inkey()` bit-index handling, reusing `_set_attr_nick` in `_set_nick_color`, removing duplicated word-navigation zero checks, simplifying delete-word LDIR pointer setup, sharing the `u8_div10` decimal helper, and using `rrca` for key_ss_arrow bit-0 tests.
- HW status (2026-04-24): user reports the latest audit fixes and all three sequential shrink passes (`50_main_output.asm`, `70_input_lookup.asm`, `80_ui_runtime.asm`) have been tested on real hardware and behave OK.

## Resume Here
- The ASM root is now split: `asm/spectalk_asm.asm` is a thin root and the real code lives in ordered modules inside `asm/spectalk_asm/`.
- Keep include order stable unless you intentionally revalidate layout-sensitive ASM changes; the split was done as a contiguous cut so local `jr` ranges and code placement stay unchanged.
- The pre-split baseline is available in `Development/83_asm_split_baseline_20260422`.
- `make build` now owns the BPE preprocessing step. Use `nobpe` only when you intentionally want the non-BPE path.
- After `make`, sanity-check `git diff` before trusting `git status` on `src/*.c`: the BPE prep/restore path in this workspace can leave source-looking noise even when the real task change is only in ASM.
- Add future routines to the nearest domain module instead of growing the root file again.
- `asm/divmmc_uart.asm` is still part of the active resident build outside the split module tree. Its only live local state is `_is_recv`; do not reintroduce `_poked_byte` / `_byte_buff` unless a real writer/pushback feature returns with verified call sites.
- Fresh 2026-04-23 shrink rule that paid immediately: if a resident ASM helper and all of its callees already leave `IY`/`IX` alone, drop the outer `push`/`pop` instead of preserving the register "just in case". This was verified in `_try_read_line_nodrain()`, `_reapply_screen_attributes()`, `_cls_fast()`, `_main_print_time_prefix()`, and `_read_key()`.
- Also from this pass: repeated local endings in hand-written state machines are still worth tail-merging. `_read_key()` shrank cleanly by routing the `repeat_timer` emit cases through one shared `rk_rep_emit` tail instead of repeating `ld (_repeat_timer),a / ld l,b / ret`.
- Rejected probe from this pass: `_utf8_to_ascii()` still has `u8a_store -> u8a_loop` out of `jr` range (`-$B5` in the assembler error). Do not flip that backedge blindly; only `_cls_fast() -> _reapply_screen_attributes()` came back into local-jump range.
- `main_print_wrapped_ram()` still pays most of its local size tax in the `IX`-based "last space" tracker. It is the next obvious ASM shrink target if more resident bytes are needed, but it now sits beyond the low-risk tier.
- `redraw_input_asm()` is still on the faster bulk path, but the generic-space-path experiment in `print_str64_char()` is now known-bad and should not be revived without a more careful proof for status-bar/attr behavior.
- Applied shrink opts on top of Codex pass: unified `p64_space_*` via mask-in-C (-8B), nested-djnz `_notif_clear` without `ldir` (-4B), and `dbc_mask_2sc` helper for `draw_big_char` top/bot (-9B). All three verified HW-OK on 2026-04-22.
- `40_text_numeric_screen.asm` now prefers `_ld_hl_ix4/_ld_hl_ix6` for resident cdecl loads, treats IXL/IYL booleans as zero/nonzero flags, and reuses preserved counts/pointers across adjacent draw phases instead of recomputing them.
- `print_line64_fast()` must stay visually aligned with `_print_str64_char()`: the per-char path leaves scanline 0 blank and starts glyph data at scanline 1, so the fast row renderer must do the same or recalled/history/redrawn text appears 1 pixel higher than incrementally typed text.
- `src/spectalk.c` status-bar shrink that measured well: keep `draw_indicator()` inlined at the tail of `draw_status_bar_real()` and keep `sb_pick_status()` in the early-return form; a fuller per-callsite inline of `sb_pick_status()` was previously measured worse and is not worth reviving blindly.
- `draw_status_bar_real()` also shrank well when the builder stopped materializing one-use temps: calling `has_other_mention()` directly in the branch and reading `chan_flags` directly beat cached locals (`has_mention`, then `cur_flags`) under current SDCC output.
- In `30_rendering.asm`, when a screen/attr base is already aligned to 32 bytes and the offset is provably `0..31`, prefer `add a,l / ld l,a` over `ld rr,0..31` + `add hl,rr`; this paid off in `_attr_addr()`, `_draw_indicator()`, `_print_str64_char()`, `dbc_add_col()`, and `_print_line64_fast()`.
- In `80_ui_runtime.asm`, tiny frameless wrappers shrink well when they reuse existing resident helpers without disturbing the caller's deeper saved return/context on the stack: `cfg_kv()` got smaller by stacking `_cfg_put()` args above the wrapper's saved `val`, and `sys_puts_print()` got smaller by calling `_sys_puts()` directly instead of restating its internals.
- In the same file, if an 8-bit position is simultaneously a countdown and a zero-extended offset into `_line_buffer`, prefer `ld b,0 / add hl,bc` over copying the byte into `DE`; this paid off in `wb_left_clean()` and `wb_right()`.
- Rejected after runtime regression: for frameless/callee helpers that consume a trailing packed `uint8_t`, `pop af` + `dec sp` is not a safe replacement for `pop bc/de` + `ld a,c/e`. On Z80 the packed byte lands in `F`, so `A` reads garbage from the extra absorbed byte. This specifically broke `_sb_put_u8_2d()` and likely would have miscolored `_print_big_str()`.
- `sb_put_u8_2d()` is now intentionally misnamed but smaller: both status-bar callsites are bounded by `MAX_CHANNELS=10`, so the helper may only emit one digit (`0..9`). Do not generalize it again unless a real two-digit caller appears.
- Audit follow-up (2026-04-23): resident render/output ASM must honor visible C-level contracts, not just keep byte counts low. In particular, `main_col=64` after `pagination_pause()` means "Cancelled" is protected, and `print_big_str(..., attr)` must visibly apply that attribute. The first fix cost 32 resident bytes in the current build; keep this in mind before adding more big-font behavior.
- Rejected in this pass: rewriting `draw_clock()` with fixed indexing (`fmt_buf[n]`) grew the binary by 2 bytes; keep the pointer-walk version.
- Rejected in the status-bar follow-up: the manual-loop rewrite of `extract_network_short()` grew the binary by 34 bytes, and the seemingly cleaner nested reordering of the center-section chooser inside `draw_status_bar_real()` grew it by 16 bytes.
- SNTP retry in `/server` path: up to 3 attempts with ~1s spacing, driven by `!sntp_queried`. Fix for clock-stuck-at-00:00 when ESP8266 NTP isn't yet synced on first query.
- The current stable shrink baseline for UI follow-ups is `35722B` trimmed / `35802B` TAP container / `461B` BSS slack. If `80_ui_runtime.asm` stalls, the next untouched ASM targets remain `70_input_lookup.asm` and `50_main_output.asm`.
- `save_config_ovl()` still leaves `rx_overflow=1` defensively after using `overlay_slot`, but callers now gate that discard on whether a partial line really existed before the overlay call. Do not reintroduce blanket post-overlay `rx_overflow=1` on every exit; it can eat the first valid server reply after overlays.
- Ikkle notifications now use a longer `notify()` timeout (`250` frames, about 5 seconds at 50 Hz); if that gets revisited, recheck the perceived dwell time with the slide-in animation enabled rather than only the raw frame count.
- Product-polish audit (2026-04-23): the strongest low-cost backlog from the current codebase is lightweight UX/protocol polish, not large new subsystems: persistent last-PM reply (`/reply`), outbound `/notice`, previous/next-activity window navigation, away/config-dirty hints in the main status UI, readable topic metadata (`333`), compact WHOIS formatting, and small operator niceties around INVITE/ban-list numerics. Keep deprioritizing ideas that require per-channel member caches; `irc_handlers.c` still treats that as prohibitive in 48K.
- Product direction follow-up (2026-04-23): `/reply`, outbound `/notice`, and formatted WHOIS are the current high-value polish targets. `/back` lost priority because the switcher bar already covers fast window switching. Be careful with any `@nick` shorthand: a global `@nick text` parser would collide with normal public channel mentions, so if implemented it should likely be limited to query-open/server contexts or use a non-conflicting variant.
- IRC polish implementation note (2026-04-23): the final resident-safe compromise is `/reply`, `/notice`, disconnect-side reset of `last_pm_nick`, help-text updates, and compact WHOIS rendering for `311`/`319`. A fuller WHOIS handler/table pass and local `/notice` echo both overflowed memory; keep future polish on the existing default/render/send paths unless a separate shrink pass recovers headroom.
- Status-bar regression note (2026-04-23): the bizarre counters (`0/0`, `4/4`, `7/7`) were not caused by the `idx/total` logic; the real bug was ABI breakage in `_sb_put_u8_2d()` after the packed-byte `pop af` experiment. Keep the status-bar C logic aligned with the pre-regression version unless there is a separate, independently verified UX change to make.
- Product decision (2026-04-24): do not spend resident bytes on UDG/special glyph rendering for ASCII smilies like `:)`, `;)`, `:(`, or `:O`. In 64-column text the readability gain is marginal, the parser/font hooks would consume scarce slack, and the idea should stay rejected unless a much larger shrink creates headroom and HW visuals prove it is clearly worth it.
- Bookmarks/session planning (2026-04-24): viable as a release-star MVP only if it stays zero-RAM or near-zero-RAM: save current server/port plus active non-query channels into config, parse a single startup `autojoin=`/`channels=` line into a transient post-001 join loop, and keep multi-server bookmark selection overlay-only or deferred. Do not add a resident bookmark table; BSS slack is currently too tight.
- Bookmarks/session implementation (2026-04-24): final MVP on `codex/bookmark-autojoin-shrink` saves active non-query channels as `channels=` from `!save`, saves the independent `autojoin=0|1` flag, loads the channel list into `search_pattern`, and replays it as one comma-list `JOIN` when `autojoin` is enabled. Current branch delays replay until `376` end-of-MOTD or `422` no-MOTD, with a small extra gate for NickServ auto-identify completion. `autoconnect` controls only server connection. Explicit `/server host` clears the pending autojoin. The old probe format `autojoin=#chan` is intentionally not kept for compatibility because the compatibility branch cost about 31 resident bytes; new configs must use `autojoin=1` plus `channels=#chan`. The robust variant that rereads config inside `/server` before TCP connect still overflows BSS and needs a prior shrink or ASM/minimal-parser rewrite.
- Help overlay pagination (2026-04-24): `src/SPECTALK_HELP.txt` currently has 48 visible lines, exactly 4 pages at `LINES_PER_PAGE=12`, and covers all primary command entries plus the direct `/0-9` window switch. `help_render_ovl()` must wrap `help_page >= total_pages` before calculating `target_line`; otherwise pressing a key on page 4 renders a blank page 5 because EOF is hit exactly at a page boundary. Current `make`: resident unchanged at `36179B`, `SPCTLK1.OVL` is `1396B`.

## Patterns
- [`fixed-numeric-asm-probe.md`](patterns/fixed-numeric-asm-probe.md): short numeric/error probes inside scans can shrink as local naked ASM when the old C already read the same bytes and the helper returns a compact class/boolean.
- [`fixed-token-asm-advance.md`](patterns/fixed-token-asm-advance.md): fixed-token matchers can return the advanced pointer directly when the caller immediately needs bytes after the token, avoiding a second C pointer add after a boolean match.
- [`fixed-token-asm-match.md`](patterns/fixed-token-asm-match.md): one-off C chains that compare many fixed token bytes can shrink as a local fastcall naked ASM loop over a `DEFM` key when the pointer contract is already bounded/tokenized.
- [`irc-tokenized-param-copy.md`](patterns/irc-tokenized-param-copy.md): after `irc_params_ensure()`, params are in-place NUL-terminated tokens; bounded copies can use `st_copy_n()` directly instead of re-scanning for spaces.
- [`progressive-size-optimization-worktree.md`](patterns/progressive-size-optimization-worktree.md): size work in `codex/size-opt-progressive` must be measured, one logical change per commit, build-verified with HW pending, and reversible by commit.
- [`irc-core-glirc-feature-triage.md`](patterns/irc-core-glirc-feature-triage.md): when mining `irc-core`/`glirc` for ideas, prefer small protocol-correctness imports such as STATUSMSG routing and measured send-rate/MODE helpers; do not import desktop-client model features into resident code.
- [`raw-udp-ntp-fallback.md`](patterns/raw-udp-ntp-fallback.md): old ESP AT firmware can still sync time by raw UDP NTP before IRC TCP opens; keep the code in SPCTLK6 and do not use `ring_buffer` for RX while an overlay executes.
- [`traffic-notif-admin-routing.md`](patterns/traffic-notif-admin-routing.md): `!traffic` gates only JOIN/PART/QUIT presence text; KICK/MODE/ban/admin messages route through `notify()` and classic inline notify output keeps timestamp/wrap indent.
- [`input-cursor-shift-arrow-contract.md`](patterns/input-cursor-shift-arrow-contract.md): cursor caps indicator uses cached shift state so CAPS SHIFT+arrow navigation does not flash the cursor between scanlines.
- [`irc-fallback-render-contract.md`](patterns/irc-fallback-render-contract.md): fallback IRC output is still real traffic; keep it visible but timestamped/indented instead of dropping or printing raw at column 0.
- [`render-scroll-external-llm-triage.md`](patterns/render-scroll-external-llm-triage.md): consolidated DeepSeek/Claude/Gemini render-scroll/RX optimization triage; use this as the starting order for future prototypes and to avoid retrying rejected ideas.
- [`resident-history-switcher-shrink.md`](patterns/resident-history-switcher-shrink.md): command-history BSS, switcher tab rendering, and CTCP literal shrink wins/rejections measured on the current resident build.
- [`divmmc-sd-io-optimization.md`](patterns/divmmc-sd-io-optimization.md): divMMC/esxDOS speed work should first optimize `F_READ`/`F_SEEK` shape, then only consider raw `DISK_READ` with a validated sector map; do not confuse this with NextZXOS `DISK_FILEMAP` streaming.
- [`names-count-asm-helper.md`](patterns/names-count-asm-helper.md): keep NAMES line counting in a small ASM helper when replacing SDCC loops; preserve the old `1 + spaces` semantics unless `/names` count behavior is intentionally changed.
- [`utf8-sanitize-fused-strip.md`](patterns/utf8-sanitize-fused-strip.md): display text sanitization is fused into `_utf8_to_ascii`; do not reintroduce a separate `_strip_irc_codes` pass without proving a net win.
- [`paginated-list-channel-message-suppression.md`](patterns/paginated-list-channel-message-suppression.md): manual `/names` owns the main area while `show_names_list` is set, filters non-NAMES traffic centrally, and renders `353` replies as fixed-width nick cells via ASM instead of raw wrapped text.
- [`bss-ldir-size-one-guard.md`](patterns/bss-ldir-size-one-guard.md): CRT zero-fill must guard `size == 1` as well as `size == 0`, because `LDIR` with `BC=0` wraps into a full 65536-byte transfer on Z80.
- [`esxdos-ix-buffer-load.md`](patterns/esxdos-ix-buffer-load.md): esxDOS buffer pointers can load directly with `ld ix, (_esx_buf)` in the current assembler, avoiding `HL` plus stack shuttles while preserving `IX`.
- [`numeric-window-slot-contract.md`](patterns/numeric-window-slot-contract.md): `/0`..`/9` and switcher direct numeric keys address physical channel slots, matching the number rendered in the tab label; do not reinterpret them as visible ordinal positions.
- [`prompt-capture-termination.md`](patterns/prompt-capture-termination.md): prompt-wait helpers that capture serial data into `rx_line` must NUL-terminate the capture on both timeout and prompt-success exits if callers may inspect the buffer.
- [`whatsnew-release-assets.md`](patterns/whatsnew-release-assets.md): `!changelog` content is generated from `release/version.txt`, `release/changes.txt`, and `release/logo.png`; keep the final change line as the magenta catch-all and rebuild to verify SPCTLK3 headroom.
- [`connect-retry-prompt-spacing.md`](patterns/connect-retry-prompt-spacing.md): connection failure prompts should rely on `ui_err()`/`main_print()` already ending the error line; do not add a second newline before `prompt_yn("Retry (y/n)?")`, but keep the newline before an accepted retry attempt.
- [`irc-long-session-count-resync.md`](patterns/irc-long-session-count-resync.md): in multi-channel IRC sessions, `QUIT` cannot be attributed without member lists; keep exact single-channel decrement and do not auto-run NAMES in very large channels unless there is an explicit idle/manual strategy.
- [`public-github-snapshot-sync.md`](patterns/public-github-snapshot-sync.md): the public GitHub clone has a separate release-history line; sync it from dev as a snapshot while preserving public docs/images, track `release/about_earth/*.bin`, verify with `make release NO_COLOR=1`, and do not push unless explicitly asked.
- [`brand-version-string-contract.md`](patterns/brand-version-string-contract.md): UI-facing app/version strings should use `SpecTalkZX 1.3.8` style, with `ZX` attached and no leading `v` before the numeric version.
- [`divmmc-uart-zxuno-port-toggle.md`](patterns/divmmc-uart-zxuno-port-toggle.md): ZX-Uno UART uses `C=$3B` with `B=$FC` as address port and `B=$FD` as data/register port, so adjacent port accesses can toggle with `inc b`/`dec b` when no call or clobber intervenes.
- [`divmmc-sd-card-diagnostics.md`](patterns/divmmc-sd-card-diagnostics.md): when Windows can list an esxDOS SD but divMMC cannot use it, check partition metadata before file contents; `Offset=0`, superfloppy layouts, GPT/exFAT, extended partitions, or a partition type/filesystem mismatch are stronger suspects than visible `/SYS`/`/BIN` names.
- [`asm-root-include-split.md`](patterns/asm-root-include-split.md): keep the resident ASM as a thin ordered root with contiguous domain modules so large refactors stay reviewable without disturbing code layout.
- [`build-target-preprocess-deps.md`](patterns/build-target-preprocess-deps.md): any direct build target must own the preprocessing it needs and track include/module inputs explicitly, leaving bypasses as opt-in targets.
- [`bounded-string-copy-terminator.md`](patterns/bounded-string-copy-terminator.md): bounded Z80 string copies can write the source byte before testing for NUL only when the terminator path returns immediately and the count-exhausted path still appends a safety NUL.
- [`rx-ring-line-parser-contract.md`](patterns/rx-ring-line-parser-contract.md): ring heads/tails are 0..2047 offsets, line parser helpers rely on `rx_pos`/`rx_last_len` being 16-bit, and overflow discard paths must avoid stale stack cleanup.
- [`irc-mode-wrapper.md`](patterns/irc-mode-wrapper.md): simple IRC wrappers should prefer passthrough semantics with only the minimum implicit target logic needed for convenience, but query numerics should still produce a visible reply.
- [`irc-format-strip-contract.md`](patterns/irc-format-strip-contract.md): IRC formatting stripping relies on digit tests returning carry set for digits, and trailing text must be isolated before parameter tokenization.
- [`resident-irc-polish-budget.md`](patterns/resident-irc-polish-budget.md): resident IRC niceties should piggyback on existing send/render paths; dedicated helpers and numeric dispatch entries are often too expensive once BSS slack is tight.
- [`outgoing-pm-query-activation.md`](patterns/outgoing-pm-query-activation.md): explicit `/msg nick text` should activate the target query before sending so the local echo appears in the PM window, while generic private send helpers remain navigation-neutral unless the caller opts in.
- [`cold-command-overlay-shrink.md`](patterns/cold-command-overlay-shrink.md): cold local commands can move display-only work to SPCTLK1 when the resident wrapper preserves RX partial-line discard and the overlay resets ring/rx cursors before returning.
- [`config-bookmarks-zero-ram.md`](patterns/config-bookmarks-zero-ram.md): IRC bookmarks/session restore should be represented in config and replayed through existing connect/JOIN paths without a resident bookmark table.
- [`autojoin-handshake-gate.md`](patterns/autojoin-handshake-gate.md): restored-session autojoin should wait for the IRC handshake's user-visible end (`376`/`422`) and for any in-flight auto-identify acknowledgement before sending pending `JOIN`.
- [`resident-asm-dead-local-state.md`](patterns/resident-asm-dead-local-state.md): if a tiny resident ASM helper keeps local BSS state that no in-tree code writes anymore, remove the dead branch and then collapse the public wrapper around the helper's actual return contract.
- [`resident-asm-preserve-tail-merge.md`](patterns/resident-asm-preserve-tail-merge.md): in resident ASM, drop `IX/IY` saves that neither the helper nor its callees need, then tail-merge repeated tiny return blocks before attempting riskier structural rewrites.
- [`resident-fixed-page-scratch.md`](patterns/resident-fixed-page-scratch.md): use documented transient printer-buffer tail bytes and fixed-page low-byte bounds only when the live range and page invariant are explicit.
- [`resident-parser-state-machine-shrink.md`](patterns/resident-parser-state-machine-shrink.md): shrink resident parser state machines by chaining fixed-length skip tails, moving common exits to unlock `jr`, and replacing repeated pointer save/restore with a temp pointer register only when state registers stay explicit.
- [`resident-asm-register-lifetime-shrink.md`](patterns/resident-asm-register-lifetime-shrink.md): micro-shrink register rewrites are acceptable when the register lifetime is explicit and later uses, especially `DE` as a 16-bit offset, cannot inherit stale high bytes.
- [`single-byte-callee-popaf.md`](patterns/single-byte-callee-popaf.md): `pop af` is not a safe way to extract a packed trailing `uint8_t` argument into `A` in `__z88dk_callee` helpers; use `pop bc/de` plus `ld a,c/e` instead.
- [`help-text-source.md`](patterns/help-text-source.md): command help that ships inside `SPECTALK.DAT` should come from a tracked text source, not from hand-edited local DAT payloads.
- [`notification-builder-helpers.md`](patterns/notification-builder-helpers.md): deduplicate short notification builders by arity, but only keep the helper if `make` proves a net byte win.
- [`notification-timeout-animation-guard.md`](patterns/notification-timeout-animation-guard.md): notification slide-in must be gated by a live timeout as well as position, because overlays can cancel the row while private animation counters remain stale.
- [`part-notification-replace.md`](patterns/part-notification-replace.md): channel leave notifications must cancel the current footer notification, and any prefix routed through `notify2()` must stay out of BPE unless that builder explicitly expands tokens.
- [`disconnect-confirmation-guard.md`](patterns/disconnect-confirmation-guard.md): commands that tear down an active connection should share the same guarded `y/n` confirmation helper instead of open-coding input loops.
- [`display-only-latin1-glyph.md`](patterns/display-only-latin1-glyph.md): display-only Spanish `ñ` uses internal byte `127`, with UTF-8 `Ñ`/`ñ` mapped there and the generated DAT font slot patched by the BPE build step.
- [`local-artifacts-gitignore.md`](patterns/local-artifacts-gitignore.md): local tooling files, backups and build outputs that are not part of the shipped program should be hidden via `.gitignore`, not left as noisy untracked entries.
- [`codex-rg-windowsapps-shim.md`](patterns/codex-rg-windowsapps-shim.md): when Codex's packaged `rg.exe` is blocked by `WindowsApps`, install or copy a normal `rg.exe` into a user PATH directory instead of changing AppX ACLs.
- [`skill-progressive-disclosure-evals.md`](patterns/skill-progressive-disclosure-evals.md): if a large Codex skill keeps giving shallow audits or dedup-only shrink passes, keep the main `SKILL.md` short and move the mode detail into references/scripts plus a forward-test corpus built from real project cases.
- [`asm-render-contract-guards.md`](patterns/asm-render-contract-guards.md): output/render ASM wrappers must re-check cancellation sentinels after `_main_newline()` and must either honor attribute parameters or make the caller pre-fill contract explicit.
- [`status-clock-overlay-tick.md`](patterns/status-clock-overlay-tick.md): status-bar clock updates must stay in the common main-loop tick path, outside overlay-specific branches, and draw only after minute/hour wrap is finalized.
- [`double-height-bright-split.md`](patterns/double-height-bright-split.md): double-height 64-col text must force BRIGHT on for the upper attribute row and BRIGHT off for the lower row, preserving theme ink/paper bits.
- [`about-theme-adaptive-earth.md`](patterns/about-theme-adaptive-earth.md): `!about` Earth must combine generated ink/bright with active theme PAPER, use green/BRIGHT shading for theme 2, and avoid literal black/white about clears outside theme 1.
- [`overlay-about-keepalive.md`](patterns/overlay-about-keepalive.md): during `ABOUT`, bypass `ring_buffer` with a bounded UART-to-`rx_line` pump that calls the normal parser, while Earth ticks read frame packets from SPCTLK2 init-only dead code instead of clobbering `rx_line`.
- [`overlay-bitmap-animation-budget.md`](patterns/overlay-bitmap-animation-budget.md): full bitmap animation data does not fit in a 2048B executable overlay; reduce/repack aggressively or stream data while preserving `OVERLAY_ABOUT` keepalive/exit behavior.
- [`about-disk-filemap-streaming.md`](patterns/about-disk-filemap-streaming.md): NextZXOS `DISK_FILEMAP`/`DISK_STRMSTART` can accelerate about frame reads only as a probe-gated path with 512B sector-aligned packets and `F_READ` fallback.
- [`overlay-exit-rx-reset.md`](patterns/overlay-exit-rx-reset.md): overlay exit paths must discard parser/ring state if `ring_buffer` has been reused as overlay code storage.
- [`overlay-save-fragment-discard.md`](patterns/overlay-save-fragment-discard.md): overlays that reuse `overlay_slot` must only force post-call `rx_overflow` when a partial line already existed before the call; blanket exit-time discards can swallow the first valid reply after the overlay.
- [`overlay-slot-bounded-config-save.md`](patterns/overlay-slot-bounded-config-save.md): SPCTLK4 config writers must bound every append before it reaches past the 512-byte `overlay_slot`; a final size check is not enough once memory has already been overwritten.
- [`overlay-resident-string-dedup.md`](patterns/overlay-resident-string-dedup.md): overlays should reuse resident exported string constants when the text is identical, to recover overlay headroom without changing UI or growing TAP.
- [`overlay-entry-rebalance.md`](patterns/overlay-entry-rebalance.md): cold independent overlay entries can move between SPCTLK blocks when measured as resident-free literal changes, but do not split entries that directly call each other or load overlays from inside overlays.
- [`overlay-cold-status-text-shrink.md`](patterns/overlay-cold-status-text-shrink.md): established user-facing overlay labels/status words must not be shortened for byte savings without explicit approval.
- [`z80-ldai-iff-save.md`](patterns/z80-ldai-iff-save.md): avoid `ld a,i` IFF save/restore in routines that can tolerate a fixed interrupt state, and document the callsite contract when doing so.
- [`overlay-local-helper-relocation.md`](patterns/overlay-local-helper-relocation.md): if a helper is only imported by one overlay, first free overlay headroom, then move the helper into that overlay and remove it from the resident ABI.
- [`fast-text-renderer-alignment.md`](patterns/fast-text-renderer-alignment.md): any bulk 64-col row renderer must reproduce the same scanline padding as the per-character renderer, or redrawn text will jump vertically relative to incrementally printed text and the cursor/prompt.
- [`frameless-asm-helper-reuse.md`](patterns/frameless-asm-helper-reuse.md): small resident frameless wrappers should call an existing helper instead of inlining the same byte loop again when the helper's callee stack contract can sit above the wrapper's deeper saved context without disturbing it.
- [`resident-asm-helper-reuse.md`](patterns/resident-asm-helper-reuse.md): in resident hand-written ASM, prefer shared IX load helpers and preserved register reuse over open-coded re-materialization when the callee contract already proves the values are still live.
- [`rendering-hotpath-byte-rules.md`](patterns/rendering-hotpath-byte-rules.md): for rendering hot paths, exploit proven alignment/caching contracts, collapse byte-packed coordinate adds into 16-bit adds, and do not pay `IY` save/restore or cache revalidation that the callee contract already makes unnecessary.
- [`external-review-context-package.md`](patterns/external-review-context-package.md): share packages for external review should include a reusable prompt, preserve relative paths, and stay scoped to current active source plus relevant `.mex` constraints.
- [`demoscene-render-scroll-review.md`](patterns/demoscene-render-scroll-review.md): demoscene-inspired render/scroll ideas should be measurement-first; the current accepted low-risk changes are `_print_line64_fast()` blank-pair skipping and direct row-19 scroll clear, stack/SMC/HALT/smooth-scroll remain prototype-only, and dual unpacked-font proposals must not steal `_ring_buffer`/printer-page memory without an explicit experimental feature cut.
- [`aggressive-z80-proposal-triage.md`](patterns/aggressive-z80-proposal-triage.md): external byte/T-state tricks must be classified by target compatibility, ABI/stack safety, interrupt/esxDOS contracts, and measured build impact before entering resident code.
- [`bpe-safe-shared-string-dedup.md`](patterns/bpe-safe-shared-string-dedup.md): screen-only repeated C strings can be pooled as `S_` constants only when `tools\bpe_build.py` also marks them safe for `SB_` renaming/compression; UART/protocol strings must stay uncompressed.
- [`overlay-exported-resident-constants.md`](patterns/overlay-exported-resident-constants.md): strings or helpers that look dead in resident C may still be exported to overlays through `gen_overlay_defs.py`; check overlay imports before purging.
- [`irc-parser-space-split-fastpath.md`](patterns/irc-parser-space-split-fastpath.md): IRC parser command-token splits can use local fastcall ASM that NUL-terminates the current token and skips separators in one pass; treat control/space bytes `1..32` as separators and skip following `<=32` bytes so polluted numerics still dispatch through the numeric table instead of `h_default_cmd()`.
- [`resident-channel-reset-ldir.md`](patterns/resident-channel-reset-ldir.md): hand-ASM `LDIR` channel resets can measure smaller, but this project has a prior HW rollback for ASM reset/defrag corruption; keep the C reset unless a focused hardware reconnect/switcher/status test passes.
- [`bpe-aware-main-print-fastpath.md`](patterns/bpe-aware-main-print-fastpath.md): `main_print()` short-line fast paths must preserve the BPE-aware slow path by treating any byte `>=0x80` as a forced `_main_puts()` case.
- [`aggressive-pre-render-shrink.md`](patterns/aggressive-pre-render-shrink.md): before spending resident bytes on render/scroll experiments, recover slack through measured dead-code, ABI-narrowing, fixed-scratch, and small ASM rewrites, keeping rejected byte economics visible.
- [`sntp-retry-on-connect.md`](patterns/sntp-retry-on-connect.md): the `/server` connect path must retry `AT+CIPSNTPTIME?` up to 3 times with a delay, because the ESP8266 can return a `1970` placeholder before NTP has actually resolved; retries must use `sntp_queried` as the exit signal, stay inside the AT-command window, and honor `BREAK` across all attempts.
- [`rtc-time-source.md`](patterns/rtc-time-source.md): valid RTC time is an opt-in local source represented only by `sntp_tz==TZ_RTC`; skip SNTP/TZ application in that mode, clear back to numeric TZ on seed failure, and show `RTC` in user-facing timezone UI.
- [`cold-time-source-naked-asm-shrink.md`](patterns/cold-time-source-naked-asm-shrink.md): tiny cold time-source wrappers can be naked ASM when they preserve UART strings, RTC/SNTP gates, `!tz` dispatch semantics, and `rx_overflow` behavior exactly.
- [`keyboard-translation-table-shrink.md`](patterns/keyboard-translation-table-shrink.md): `_in_inkey()` should keep the explicit CAPS table unless a measured replacement beats it; deriving uppercase plus a small exception table currently grows the resident binary.
- [`input-cache-vram-attr.md`](patterns/input-cache-vram-attr.md): input redraw caching should cache characters only and validate attributes against real VRAM; the old fixed-RAM attribute cache was write-only.
- [`timestamp-indent-fastpath.md`](patterns/timestamp-indent-fastpath.md): the main timestamp/wrap indent is currently a fixed 6-column contract; shared direct clear helpers are valid only while every writer keeps `wrap_indent` to 0 or 6.
- [`i2c-bitbang-restore-ei.md`](patterns/i2c-bitbang-restore-ei.md): software-timed I2C blocks must `ei` after the last bus transition and before returning, otherwise the DI leaks through overlay return into the next `frame_wait`.
